<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">정략결혼이라고는 해도 확실한 애정이 두 사람에게는 있다고 이유도 없이 확신하고 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여자로서의 애정이 강한 한편 가족애는 극히 희박</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">좋은 의미는 나쁜 의미든 사랑으로밖에 살수 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사랑이 끝난다면 자신도 끝나는 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이건 다음 권에서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">!</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코는 시해선이 되려고 했지만 후토의 모략에 의해 굽지 않은 항아리에 영혼을 담아버려 실패해 원령이 됐다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 토지코와 토지코노이라츠메는 동일 인물이 아니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">신주 인터뷰에도 있음</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; clear: none; float: none;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;">●</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box;">소가노 토지코는 무엇을 말하지 않는가</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/003.jpg"/></p>
<p style="text-align: left; clear: none; float: none;"><br/></p>
<p class="moreless_fold" id="more2028_2"><span onclick="toggleMoreLess(this, '2028_2','토요사토미미노 미코','접기'); return false;" style="cursor: pointer;">토요사토미미노 미코</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/004.jpg"/></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사에서는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">잘 알고 계시는 쇼토쿠 태자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">우마야도 황자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">厩戸皇子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">비다쓰 천황 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">3</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">월 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(574</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">월 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">7</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">) ~ </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스이코 천황 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">30</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">월 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">22</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(622</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">4</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">월 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">8</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">). </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요메이 천황의 제 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">황자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스이코 천황의 섭정</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">근래에는 허구설도 눈에 띈다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">우마야도 왕</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">厩戸王</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이라는 인물은 실재했지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">지금 말하는 쇼토쿠 태자는 거기서 창작된 거라는 내용이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이건 당시의 문헌을 엄밀하게 정밀조사 해본 결과</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자 전설에 관련된 기술은 거의 제외되어 버린 것에서 유래한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자세한 것은 직접 조사하자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자의 불교 관계의 일화가 몹시 많고 모두 엉뚱하고 말도 안 되는 것이기에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">대부분 과장됐을 것이라는 건 실재</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">허구설 관계없이 자주 있는 의견</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">실재설 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">vs </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">허구설의 쟁점은 이카루가궁</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">斑鳩宮</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 살고 있었다는 우마야도 왕이 실제로 쇼토쿠 태자에 필적하는 정도의 권력과 지위를 가지고 있었다는 부분에 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">즉 일개 왕족인 그를 모델로 했을 뿐인 창작인지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아니면 정말로 황태자나 섭정으로서의 실적을 가진 그를 칭하는 이야기에 호화로운 꼬리와 지느러미가 붙었느냐 하는 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이름과 소가 가문의 혈통만 빌려 일본의 정치와 종교에 깊게 관여한 쇼토쿠 태자라는 인물을 만들었다고 한다면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그건 이미 우마야도 왕과는 다른 사람이라고 할 수 있을 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">예를 들자면 동방계 사이에 미코는 쇼토쿠 태자와 동일하다고 해도 문제는 없지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사학이나 정치사를 말하는데 있어서 동일인물로서 미코를 꺼내들면 빈축을 사는 일이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어느 쪽이든</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교를 퍼트리는데 표방해야할 카리스마로서 많은 덧붙임 설정과 과장이 더해져 현재의 태자신앙이 되었다는 것은 상상하기 쉽다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자라는 이름은 살아있을 적에는 사용하지 않았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">처음 나온 것은 사후 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">100</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년이 지나고 나온 현존하는 가장 오래된 한시집</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">漢詩集</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">회풍조</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">懐風藻</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 전해진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코노이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">刀自古郎女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">], </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">우지노카이타코노히메미코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">菟道貝蛸皇女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">], </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">타치바나노오오이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">橘大郎女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">], </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">膳部菩岐</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">々</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">美郎女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">작품 내에서는 카시와데노미노이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">膳美郎女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 아내로 두고 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">14</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명의 아이가 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가 가문과 천황 가문의 혈통</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">할아버지는 킨메이 천황이며 소가노 우마코의 동생 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명과 결혼하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">각각 쇼토쿠 태자의 아버지인 요메이 천황과 어머니인 아나호베노하시히토노히메미코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">穴穂部間人皇女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 낳았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">두 사람의 배다른 남매혼에 의해 태어난 것이 우마야도 황자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">즉 쇼토쿠 태자이므로</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천황가와 소가 가문의 하프라고 할 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 우마코는 증조할아버지에 해당되며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코노이라츠메는 사촌이 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그렇기 때문에 소가 가문은 적극적으로 태자를 번창시켜 권력을 얻었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">10</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명의 말을 동시에 알아들었다는 것에서 토요사토미미</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">豊聡耳</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 불린다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">단 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">10</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명분을 순서대로 연속해서 듣고 각각 대답했다고 하는 설도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또한 상국성덕법왕제설</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">上宮聖徳法王帝説</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에서는 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">8</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명이며 우마야토노토요야츠미미노미코토</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">厩戸豊聰八耳命</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 팔</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">八</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">은 다수라는 의미의 가능성도 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">남의 이야기를 잘 듣고 이해하는 것에서 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">굉장히 머리가 좋다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 의미가 기본이고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">실제로 이야기를 들은 부분은 나중에 생긴 과장이라고도 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어머니인 하시히토 황녀</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">間人皇女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 태내에 구세관음</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">救世觀音</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 들어가 임신한 아이이며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">마구간 앞에서 태어났다고 하지만 대륙 문화 유입에 의해 나중에 만들어진 것이라고도 전해지고 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">탄생지의 지명이 우마야도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">혹은 소가노 우마코의 저택에서 태어났다고 하는 설도 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">탄생과 사망 그 외에 중요한 고비가 반드시 소의 해이기에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">허구감도 빚어낸다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교를 독실이 숭배하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">서민을 포함해 일본에서 불교가 퍼질 토대가 되었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">죽기 직전에 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 세상은 가짜고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">부처만이 진짜다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 아내인 타치바나노오오이라츠메에게 말했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">和</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">を</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">以</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">て</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">貴</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">しと</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">為</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">し</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">、</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">忤</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">ふること</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">無</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">きを</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">宗</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">とせよ</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">。』</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">로 시작하는 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">17</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">조의 헌법의 작성자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">와</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">和</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 글자는 사전적인 평화나 조화의 억누름이라기보다는 사람들이 유연하게 사이좋게 지내고 이야기 나누는 상태의 의미라 여겨진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다른 의견을 배척하지 않고 부드럽고 친하게 지내자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교나 유교의 영향을 강하게 받았으며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">예를 들면 이 문장도 공자의 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">논어</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">예지용화위귀</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">禮之用和爲貴</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가 근본</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">제 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">조에는 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">독실하게 삼보를 읊어라</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">삼보란 불</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">佛</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">법</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">法</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">승</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">僧</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이니</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">篤</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">く</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">三宝</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">を</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">敬</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">へ</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">。</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">三宝</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">とは</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">仏 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">· </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">法 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">僧</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">なり</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">。</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 되어있듯이 불교에 대한 마음은 특히 강하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카타오카 산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">片岡山</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">기인 설화</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. 613</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">12</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">월 태자는 카타오카 산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">나라현 키타카스라기 군오지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">奈良県北葛城郡王寺町</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 유행</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">遊行</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하러 갔을 때 굶으며 누워있던 사람을 발견해 옷과 밥을 준 다음 노래를 읊었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다음날 그 기인</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">飢人</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">은 죽어있었고 이를 슬퍼한 태자는 정중하게 묻어주었지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">며칠이 지난 후 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역시 그 사람은 평범한 인간이 아닌 성인</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">聖人</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">임이 틀림없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 무덤을 조사시킨다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그러자 무덤은 텅 비어있었고 태자가 준 옷이 관 위에 개여 놓여있었으며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자는 그 옷을 다시 입었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">상궁성덕태자전보궐기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">上宮聖徳太子伝補闕記</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에서는 기인을 갸름하고 큰 머리</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">귀가 길며 눈은 가늘다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">눈을 보면 안에 사람이 아닌 금빛을 가지고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">별난 인상을 가졌다고 묘사한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">더불어 그 주위에는 몹시 향기로운 냄새가 자욱했다고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">문헌에 따라 기인의 용모는 변화한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">향기하면 마찬가지로 상궁성덕태자전보궐기에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어릴 적 태자 역시 형언할 수 없는 좋은 향기를 내</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">한 번 안으면 몇 개월은 그 향기가 남아있었다고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자가 죽은 후</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">막을 것이 없어진 소가 가문은 드디어 권력을 독점한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">죠메이 천황</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">타무라 황자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 다음은 아내인 고교쿠 천황이 왕의 자리에 이른다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코의 오라비인 소가노 에미시는 조정의 허가를 얻지 않고 장남인 이루카를 대신</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">大臣</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">으로</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">차남</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베노 오오오미</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">物部大臣</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고밖에 안 쓰여있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 모노노베 측의 대신으로 임명했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이건 에니시의 어머니가 모노노베노 모리야의 동생</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후츠히메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이었기 때문</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이루카는 소가의 혈통을 잇는 후루히토노 오에 황자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">古人大兄皇子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 차기 천황으로 세우기 위해 대립후보인 야마시로노 오에 왕</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">山背大兄王</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 사는 이카루가 궁을 공격한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이코마 산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">生駒山</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">으로 도망친 야마시로노 오에 왕은 신하에게 이대로 동국으로 도망쳐 재기하는 것을 권유받지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">백성을 고통스럽게 하기 때문에 거절</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이카루가 사에 돌아가 황자와 아내와 함께 자살</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기에 쇼토쿠 태자의 혈통을 잇는 상궁왕가</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">上宮王家</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 단절된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 일은 에미시도 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자신의 신변을 위협할거다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 이루카를 비난</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가 가문 타도의 공기도 강해진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">645</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 소가노 이루카는 나카노 오에 황자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">中大兄皇子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 의해 고교쿠 천황</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">皇極天皇</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 어전에서 암살당해 빗속에 유체를 방치 당한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 쿠데타를 을사의 변이라고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 후 에미시도 저택에 방화를 당해 죽는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이걸로 천황가와 이어지는 권세를 잃은 소가 가문은 거의 자멸이라는 형태로 몰락하여 역사로부터 모습을 감추게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">작품 내에서는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">神子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">와 가장 발음이 가까운 천황가의 남자 아이라는 것을 나타내는 황자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">皇子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 토요사토미미</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">豊聡耳</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">뒤에 붙였다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">생전에는 남자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시해선이 되어 부활했을 때는 여성이 되었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">생전의 기억은 희미하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코에 대해서도 사실 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소중한 아내였을 것</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이라는 사실관계밖에 기억하지 못한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원작에서는 생전에 욕망을 듣는 힘이 있었는지 미묘하지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기서는 노병에 의한 능력의 상실과 세이가의 음모</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자세한 것은 다음 장</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">로 애매해진 것으로 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카타오카 산에서 만난 선녀인 세이가에게 도교의 가르침을 받고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">같이 도교를 신앙하고 있던 후토히메와 공모하여 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">587</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 종교전쟁을 일으킨다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">실제 기인전설의 연대와 어긋난다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 때가 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">13</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 태자는 세이가의 사심</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">邪心</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">을 느꼈기 때문에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그녀 없이 수행하기로 결의</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가르침을 받을 수 있는 이가 이 나라에는 없었고 수행은 난항으로 치닫게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">수행에 쓰인 약의 독성으로 몸을 망가트리고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">귀의 힘까지 잃어버린다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불로는 어렵게 달성했지만 불사는 아무리 노력해도 되지 못했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 결과 세이가에게 의지하게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">종교전쟁은 모노노베 가문을 궁지에 몰아넣기 위해 아버지인 요메이 천황의 임종을 감지하여 이용했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">계략을 위해 우마코의 아내이며 토지코의 어머니인 여자를 죽이기로 했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세이가가 알고 있는 옛 태자는 아무래도 무대가 된 시대와는 상당히 다른 모양이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아내를 진심으로 소중히 여기고 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코노이라츠메도 카시와데노미노이라츠메도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">단 카시와데노미노이라츠메의 곁에 있는 경우가 더 많다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">죽음에 대한 강한 두려움</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교의 길을 추구한 결과</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교는 나를 구원해주지 않는다는 결론에 이르러 절망이 그를 도교로 향하게 했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교는 지금 와서는 정치의 도구정도로밖에 생각하고 있지 않다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">귀의 힘에 의지해왔던 만큼</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">힘을 잃어버리게 되고 나서는 남의 마음을 간파하지 못하고 타인을 믿기 힘들어졌다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">필연적으로</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">조용히 혼자서 일을 해결하려고 하게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코조차도 후토와 세이가가 이것저것 불어넣고 있다는 것을 알게 되고 나서는 마음을 터놓고 이야기하지 못하고 고뇌한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">지금은 보통사람보다도 서투른 성인의 만년</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">晩年</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">].</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기부터는 다음권에서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">!</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자의 진의</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자의 과거</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">두 아내와의 관계</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px; text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;'><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/005.jpg"/></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px; text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;'><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/006.jpg"/></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'></p>
<p class="moreless_fold" id="more2028_3"><span onclick="toggleMoreLess(this, '2028_3','모노노베노 후토','접기'); return false;" style="cursor: pointer;">모노노베노 후토</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/007.jpg"/></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사에서는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후츠히메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">布都姫</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또는 후토히메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">太暖</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 이름으로 모노노베노 모리야의 동생으로 쓰여 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">주로 소가노 우마코의 아내로서 기술된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">기씨가첩</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">紀氏家牒</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">], </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">석상진신궁략초</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">石上振神宮略抄</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에서는 소가노 우마코의 아내라고 되어있지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">구사본기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">旧事本紀</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에서는 카마히메오오토지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">鎌姫大刀自</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가 그 위치에 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">구사본기는 소가노 우마코와 쇼토쿠 태자가 지은 것으로 되어있지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후세에 미토 미츠쿠니 공</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">水戸光圀公</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이나 모토오리 노리나가</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">本居宣長</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 의해</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">전체적으로 고사기와 일본서기 등을 이어붙인 가짜임을 인정</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">단 니기하야히노미코토의 기술이 제법 많고 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">3, 5, 10</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">권은 독자적인 기재이기 때문에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">현존하지 않는 모노노베 가문의 자료의 인용이 아닌가 하는 역사적 가치를 가진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일본서기에서는 모리야의 동생에 우마코에게 시집간 무명의 인물이 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 인물은 소가 가문을 부추겨 모노노베 가문을 멸망시키고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자신의 혈족이라는 것을 이유로 모노노베의 유산을 빼앗았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">구사본기에서는 일본 최고의 신궁이라고 일컫는 이소노카미 신궁의 사이구였으며 소가 가문에 시집가지 않았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사이구란 고위의 신관이며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">정진결재하여 생활하며 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년에 몇 번 신사</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">神事</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 거행한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">올리는 것은 후쓰노미타마노쓰루기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">布都御魂剣</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">](</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후츠누시는 이것의 신격</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">) </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">말고도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베 가문의 선조인 우마시마지노미코토 등이 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베 가문은 거기서 또 아버지인 니기하야히노미코토도 신앙한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
