<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후쓰노미타마노쓰루기는 이소노카미 신궁의 신체</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">神体</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">타케미카즈치는 이걸 사용해 아시하라노나카츠쿠니</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">葦原中國</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 평정했다고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쿠니유즈리를 말함</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">). </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후츠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">布都</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 사물을 자르는 효과음이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">나중에 금족지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">禁足地</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 묻히고 세월이 지난 뒤 땅에서 나왔다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">외날의 왜곡된 철로 된 검이며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, 85cm </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">정도의 길이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 이소노카미 신궁은 모노노베 가문의 무기고이기도 했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. 4</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세기에 대륙에서 바친 칠지도 역시 이소노카미 신궁에 보관되었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스펠에 있는 오오모노이미</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">大物忌</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">란 이세 신궁</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사이구라고 하면 보통 이쪽을 가리킨다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 신관으로 때로 사이구의 대리 일도 하였으며 태양의 신인 아마테라스 오오미카미</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">天照大神</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 나타낸다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소녀에게만 맡겨져 신에게 음식을 바친다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">첫 월경이 오면 교대되지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">기본적으로는 생애독신으로 살게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아메노이와후네</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">天磐舟</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 선대 구사본기에서 니기하야히노미코토가 강림하기 위해 사용했던 하늘을 나는 배다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">별명</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아메노토리후네</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">天鳥船</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">고사기에는 타케미카즈치가 강림하는데 사용했다는 것도 이것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이와후네</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">磐舟</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 도구라고 하기보다도 그 자체가 신이며 이자나기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이자나미의 자식이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">선대 구사본기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">니기하야히노미코토는 아마테라스에게서 십종신보</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">十種神宝</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 하사받고 강림</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 중에 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">3</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">종은 삼종신기와 동일시된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이소노카미 신궁에서 모셔지고 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 십종신보를 가지고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후루노코토</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">布瑠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">の</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">言</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 주문을 외우면 죽은 사람조차 소생한다고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후루노코토는 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">히토후타미요이츠무나나야코토노타리</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후루베 유라유라토 후루베</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">一二三四五六七八九十</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">、</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">布留部由良由良止布留部</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">구사본기 제 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">5</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">권의 천손본기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">天孫本紀</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에서는 배다른 오빠 모노노베노 니에코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">物部贄子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에게 시집을 가 카마츠카</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">鎌束</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">], </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">나가에노 와쿠고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">長兄若子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">], </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">오오요시노 와쿠고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">大吉若子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">], </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카마히메노 오오토지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">鎌姫大刀自</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 낳았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">따라서 생몰년은 미상이지만 쇼토쿠 태자보다 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세대 또는 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세대 위의 인물이라고 생각된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베 가문은 니니기보다 빨리 천손강림 했다고 일컫는 니기하야히노미코토의 자손</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원래 병기를 제조관리하고 있던 가계이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">특히 지방에 혈족이 많고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이것을 야소모노노베</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">八十物部</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 칭하기도 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교전래로 소가노 우마코의 아버지이며 대신</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">大臣</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이었던 소가노 이나메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">蘇我稲目</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 숭불파로서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베노 모리야의 아버지인 모노노베노 오코시</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">物部尾輿</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 폐불파로서 싸웠다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가 가문이 숭불파를 이유로</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가 가문은 도래계</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">渡来系</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 씨족과 교우가 깊었고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그들의 선진기술을 가져 힘을 얻었기 때문이라고 생각할 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">한편 모노노베 가문은 신을 모시는 가문이었기 때문에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교의 대두로 신토가 쇠퇴하는 것 자체가 지극히 불이익</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">따라서 배불파</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">排仏派</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가 되었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 싸움은 소가노 우마코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베노 모리야 대가 되면 한 층 격화</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모리야는 절이나 불상을 파괴했고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">비구니를 알몸으로 만들어 공중에 매달아 일반인들의 면전에서 엉덩이를 채찍질하는 등의 일을 벌였다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">우마코도 역시 모리야가 차기 황위로 추천한 아나호베 황자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">穴穂部皇子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 살해</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 무력으로 모노노베 가문과 대규모 전쟁을 벌이고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모리야가 전쟁으로 죽고 종결되었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가 가문이 세운 일본 최초의 본격적 사원인 사쿠라이지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">桜井寺</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 모노노베 가문은 불태웠다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이나메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">오코시의 세대</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">대신신화전</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">大神神話伝</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 오오미와</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">大神</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">란 일본에서 제일 오래된 신사인 오오미와 신사</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">大神神社</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 나타낸다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베노 무라치</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">物部連</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 선조인 이카가시코오</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">伊香色雄</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가 세웠다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이것을 모시는 씨족이 오오미와 가문이며 후에 미와</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">三輪</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가문이 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미와 가문은 모노노베 가문</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">나카토미</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">中臣</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가문과 함께 폐불을 진행시켰다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베 가문은 종교전쟁으로 인해 몰락했지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, 686</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년부터 이소노카미 가문으로서 다시 힘을 얻는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이소노카미란 원래 후츠히메의 남편이라고 여겨지는 모노노베노 니에코를 칭했던 것이기도 하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">예를 들면 좌대신</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">左大臣</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 되어 임신의 난</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">壬申</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">の</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">乱</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에서 오토모 황자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">大友皇子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 끝까지 뒤따른 이소노카미노 마로</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">石上麻呂</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 모노노베 가문의 일족이며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">처음부터 모노노베의 성을 대고 있었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또한 구사본기에서는 니에코의 아내이기도 하면서 하쓰세베 황자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">泊瀬部皇子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">](</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스슌 천황</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">崇峻天皇</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 부인이 되었다고도 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스슌 천황은 원래 소가노 우마코의 추천을 받아 황위에 올랐지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">언제나 정치의 실권은 우마코가 쥐고 있었고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, 592</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년에는 우마코의 명령을 받아 야마토노아야노 코마</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">東漢直駒</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 의해 시역</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">弑逆</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">당함</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천황의 살해는 역사적으로도 지극히 이례적으로</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">신하에 의한 시역이 확정되어있는 천황은 유일하게 스슌 천황뿐이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자 여기서 후츠히메는 보통 우마코의 아내로 묘사된다는 것을 생각하면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후츠히메는 스슌 천황과 불륜 관계였던 게 아닐까하고 추측하는 것도 가능하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">덧붙여 토지코노이라츠메의 언니라고 하는 카와카미노이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">河上娘</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도 스슌 천황의 아내지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카와카미노이라츠메는 토지코노이라츠메와 동일시되기도 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카와카미노이라츠메는 스슌 천황 암살 후</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">암살범인 야마토노아야노 코마와 밀통이 발각되어</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">코마에게 붙잡혀 강간당했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">) </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">야마토노아야노는 우마코에게 처형당하게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일본서기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이와 같은 억측이 성립되어있는 것으로도 알 수 있지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다방면으로 후토히메의 평판은 대체로 악녀라는 점에서 일치하며 매우 심하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베 측의 기술이 많은 구사본기에서 카와히메가 우마코의 아내가 되었다고 한 것은</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">딸이라는 쿠션 하나를 두는 것으로 후토히메의 악평을 완충하는 목적일지도 모른다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">작품 내에서는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원작에서는 일단 육체를 버린 시해선은 어느 정도 원하는 모습으로 변화할 수 있지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">거의 살아있을 적의 모습을 고르겠다고 했기에 미코와는 달리 후토는 이 패턴</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">입고 있는 의복은 카리기누</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">狩衣</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">](</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스이칸</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">水千</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]). </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이건 남성만이 입는 옷이지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">예외로 후세에 나오는 가무기인</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">歌舞芸人</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 시라뵤시</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">白拍子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도 입는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에보시</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">烏帽子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도 쓰고 칼을 찬다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시라뵤시는 점차 기생으로 바뀌어가고 있었지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 유래는 무녀의 춤이라고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">실제로 사이구는 무녀 중의 무녀라고 할 수 있는 고등 여신관이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">과거의 책사로서의 행동은 세이가의 손에 의해 어딘가로 사라져버린 것일까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아니면 숨기고 있을 뿐인가 알 수 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아니</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이전부터 저랬을지도 모른다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코도 눈치 없게 그 부분을 건드리지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">건드리지 않기에 말대답은 해도 대체적으로 후토에게는 순종</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베노 모리야의 동생이며 굉장히 젊을 때 사이구가 되었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세간과 격리되어 정진결재하며 살면서 대륙에서 넘어온 도교의 서적을 발견에 들여오게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자신의 이름의 근본이 된 단검 후쓰노미타마노쓰루기를 항상 가지고 다닌다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">신체로 모셔진 쪽은 레플리카</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">). </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코가 자결하는 흉기가 되어버린 것을 후회했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교의 가르침이 사람들을 깨달음의 세계로 인도하는 것은 배에 비유한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토의 바위배</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">磐舟</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 그 배에 타지 못한 자신들을 구원해 하늘로 올라가려는 의미를 가진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자보다 빨리 불로를 달성했지만 그로 인해 너무 많은 독을 섭취해버려 몸은 너덜너덜하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여자로서의 기능도 잃었으므로 월경도 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">착실하게 마음도 망가트린 것조차 깨닫지 못하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 후에도 계속해서 선약</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">仙薬</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 실험대에 올라 한 층 더 몸을 혹사시켰다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">마지막에도 세이가의 약의 실험대가 되었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">남자나 여자라는 개념도 희박하여 연애다운 연애도 해본 적이 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여자가 아니게 되고나서는 한 층 더 성동녀</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다만 사망 시 실제 연령은 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">60</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">을 넘었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">약간 옛 말투를 쓰는 건 그것 때문</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 어조에 여성스러움이 별로 없고 남성적인 것도 심신적인 문제에서 유래된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 게야</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 우마코의 아내의 죽음과 동시에 대신 그 아내가 되었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이건 태자의 의도이기도 했지만 너무 일이 잘 풀려서 수상해했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자님은 어쩌면 단지 나를 곁에 두기 위해 그 여자를 죽인 것은 아닐까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">…… </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 생각하고는 있지만 말로는 하지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 분은 무섭고 슬픈 분이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그러다 생긴 딸은 몹시 건방지고 겁쟁이에 응석꾸러기였지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">마음에 들었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 저 쪽은 기분 나쁘게 생각하는 것 같지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">무리도 아니지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코에게 가족이라고 한 말은 평범한 결의로 쓴 말이 아니었지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사실은 어머니라고 말하고 싶었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 이젠 가족이라는 말조차 독과 같은 것이 되었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이건 다음 권에서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">!</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토의 진의</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토의 과거</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">왜 후토는 토지코를 시해선으로 만들려 하지 않았는가</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/008.jpg"/></p>
<p><br/></p>
<p class="moreless_fold" id="more2028_4"><span onclick="toggleMoreLess(this, '2028_4','카쿠 세이가','접기'); return false;" style="cursor: pointer;">카쿠 세이가</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/009.jpg"/></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사에서는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">중국의 선인</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">괴이담을 정리한 단편집 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요재지이</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">聊斎志異</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">안의 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청아</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">青娥</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">항목에 등장하는 인물</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">먼 옛날</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아주 두뇌명석하며 신동이라고 불린 곽 환</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">霍 桓</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이라는 이름의 명가 소년이 있었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">환은 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">13</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세에 당시 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">14</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세의 무 청아</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">武 青娥</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 누구와도 견줄 수 없을 정도로 아름다운 소녀에게 사랑에 빠졌다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">무 청아의 아버지는 재판관이었지만 도교에 심취해 산으로 은둔해버렸고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그녀는 그 아버지의 책을 닥치는 대로 읽어 하선고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">何仙姑</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 하는 미혼으로 남은 선인의 곁에서 동경하고 있었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">따라서 청아는 누군가에게 시집갈 생각은 전혀 없었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세상 물정을 잘 몰랐지만 평범치 않은 마음을 품은 환은 구혼하고 싶다고 어머니에게 상담하지만 청아의 평판을 알고 있던 어머니는 각하시켰다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어느 날</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그는 지나가던 도사에게 어떠한 단단한 물건이라도 슥슥 자를 수 있다는 신기한 끌을 받는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 드디어 청아의 집의 벽을 뚫고 밤에 몰래 들어간다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이불 끝까지 온 그는 세이가의 자는 얼굴을 앞에 두고 만족해</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그녀의 숨소리의 은은한 향기를 맡으면서 자신도 잠들어버린다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다음날 아침 청아와 시중인에게 도둑이라고 오해받는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">저는 도둑이 아닙니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아가씨를 너무 좋아한 나머지 곁에 있고 싶었을 뿐입니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 변명</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시중인은 그 말로 용서해 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다음에는 중매인을 보내세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라 하고 보내준다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청아는 환이 중매인을 찾아다니는걸 알고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">은근히 자신의 의향을 환의 어머니에게 전하자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그녀는 기뻐하며 중매인을 보내 구혼을 신청했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 밤에 몰래 들어간 것은 쌍방의 부모에게 알려지게 되어 양가의 사이는 악화한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청아의 어머니는 환과 그 어머니를 가문의 수치라고 심하게 매도했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">환의 어머니도 역시 거기에 분노하여</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">친척과 만날 때마다 밤에 몰래 기어든 것을 이야기했을 정도이니</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청아는 부끄러워서 죽을 것 같아 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다른 집에는 결코 시집가지 않겠다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 환의 어머니에게 맹세한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그래서 결혼과 밤에 몰래 들어간 일은 불문에 붙이고 중단</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">나중에 환의 문장에 반한 고명한 구공</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">欧公</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 중매인이 되어 양가는 화해</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청아와 환은 결혼하게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다음 해에는 맹선</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">孟仙</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이라는 아이가 태어난다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 결혼한 이후 청아는 집에 틀어박히게 되었고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아이를 돌보는 것도 유모에게 맡기고 귀여워하는 모습도 보이지 않았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 결혼 후 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">8</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 후 갑자기 청아는 가족에게 작별을 고하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 머지않아 죽어버린다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">환은 슬퍼하며 훌륭한 관에 청아를 넣어 묻었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 사실 청아는 대나무 막대를 시체로 보이게 해서 시해선이 되어</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">선계의 아버지에게 가 은거생활을 하고 있었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 다음 해 엉뚱하게도 환은 시해선인 청아와 재회한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아버지의 주선으로 환은 선계의 집에 안내받았지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">침실에 도착하자마자 청아와 뒹굴려고 했지만 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">신성한 선계를 어찌 더럽히는가</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 아버지에게 혼나 환은 쫓겨난다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">환이 원망의 말을 내뱉으며 신기한 끌로 선계로 이어지는 벼랑을 계속 파고 있을 때</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">분노한 아버지가 청아도 현세로 쫓아내버리고 만다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 후 환도 선인이 되어 두 사람은 다시 부부로서 살게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명의 아이도 낳았지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">최종적으로는 부부가 같이 모습을 감춰버린다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">무 청아</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">武 青娥</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가 곽 환</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">霍 桓</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">과 결혼하여 곽 청아</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">霍 青娥</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가 되었다고 생각된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청아가 동경한 하선고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">何仙姑</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 쇼토쿠 태자보다 후세의 인물</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시해선은 의사적으로 죽어 의대</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">依代</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 이용하여 선인이 되는 이</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 때 의대가 시체로 변하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">술이 완성하여 선인이 되면 시체는 물건으로 돌아간다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 과정을 선화</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">蝉化</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시해선이 되는 이 가운데어도 최상위 인물은 보검을 의대로 삼을 수 있으며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">陶器</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 선인의 격이 떨어진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">대나무 막대는 그 가운데서도 최저</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">운급칠첨</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">雲笈七籤</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또한 선인은 우화승천</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">羽化昇天</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하는 천인</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">산속에서 선인이 되는 지선</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">地仙</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시해선이 있지만 격은 시해선이 제일 낮다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다만 본래 선인의 개념은 시해선을 가리킨다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
