<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">동유기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">東遊記</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 있는 하선고는 어느 날 신인</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">神人</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 꿈에 신탁으로 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">운모</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">雲母</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 먹으면 몸이 가벼워지고 불사가 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 말을 들어 그걸 실천</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">확실히 몸이 가벼워지는 것을 느낀 그녀는 어머니로부터의 결혼 권유를 단호히 거절하고 산에서 놀았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후에 선인이 되는 비결을 알아 선인이 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청아가 원작에서 결혼하지 않는 것을 결의한 것은 그녀에게 동경했기 때문일 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">실제로는 조금씩 진행돼 결혼하게 되지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그렇기에 도사를 향한 꿈은 포기할 수 없었다고 여겨진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세이가가 토지코에게 보여준 독은 바곳</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">독명은 아코니틴</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">예부터 부자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">附子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 알려진 독이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">피부로도 흡수되고 입으로 섭취했을 경우 즉효성도 높다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">치사량은 체중 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1kg </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">당 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">15~16mg. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">물에는 잘 녹지 않지만 유기용매에 잘 녹는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">체내에 테트로도톡신</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(TTX) </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">감수성</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">Na+</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">채널을 활성화시키고 탈분극을 일으킨다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">말하자면 세포 레벨로 격렬한 흥분상태가 되고 마비</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">심부전</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">호흡부전 등을 일으켜 죽는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">마비독인 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">TTX</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 이론상 해독제가 되지만 약효범위가 너무 좁아 사용할 수 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다량으로 마셨을 경우는 심실세동에 의한 심부전에 이르기까지 몇 십초에서 몇 분정도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">손을 쓸 수 없는 맹독이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미량으로는 한방약도 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">한방은 도교의 강한 영향을 받고 있기에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">선인은 그에 걸맞은 약과 독의 지식을 갖고 있다고 생각된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도교 자체</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">민중을 위한 건강법이라는 측면이 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">실제로 도교의 수행법은 기를 순환시켜 심신을 건강하게 유지하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">특별한 호흡법을 하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">오곡이나 고기를 피하고 조식</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">粗食</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">을 갖고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">남녀가 마음과 몸을 주고받는 것 등이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">선인이 되는 술법에 대해 해설한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도교의 수련은 크게 내단술</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">内丹術</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">과 외단술</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">外丹術</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">로 나누어진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">내단술이란 기를 키워 체내에 단</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">丹</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">](</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불로불사의 영약</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">을 쌓아 도를 체현한 선인이 되는 것을 목표로 하는 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">수행법이 이것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">외단술이란 선단</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">仙丹</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 복용에 의한 승선</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">昇仙</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 선단의 개념은 포박자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">抱朴子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 의하면 금단</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">金丹</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">과 금액</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">金液</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이것을 만드는 것은 연단술</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">練丹術</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이라고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">금은 그 빛남과 녹슬지 않고 형태를 유지하는 신비성으로 중국에서도 귀하게 여겨졌다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 불후성</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">不朽性</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">을 거두어들이는 것이 불로불사로 이어진다고 여겨졌을 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다만 금을 그대로 섭취하는 것은 오히려 독이라고 여겨졌다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그래서 비금속</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">卑金属</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에서 금을 만들어 내 그것을 금단</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">金丹</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">으로서 복용하는 것이 좋다고 일컫는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">물론 이건 금색인 만큼 합금이기에 금 그 자체는 아니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">게다가 합금의 잡물에 비소나 수은 등의 유해한 중금속이 섞이기 쉽고 독성이 높았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또 다른 금액</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">金液</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이라고 하는 것은 금을 녹여 넣은 액체이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이것은 진짜 금을 사용했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 금은 굉장히 반응성이 부족하여 녹여서 액체로 만드는 것은 곤란</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 방법은 두 가지 정도 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그것이 수은과 청산이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이외에도 왕수나 요오드에 녹일 수 있지만 여기서는 할애한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요컨대 할로겐과 착이온을 만드는 반응</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">수은은 상온에서 액체다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 수은은 금속을 합치면 아말감이라는 액상의 합금이 되는 성질이 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 현상은 옛날부터 알려져 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도다이지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">東大寺</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 대불의 도금은 금 아말감이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">수은은 고온에서 증발하기 때문에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">금과의 합금 상태로 도포하여 가열하면 수은만이 날아가 얇은 금 도금이 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다만 당연히 수은은 유독하므로 수은 중독자를 많이 냈다고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 방법의 금액</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">金液</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">을 복용하여 불로불사가 되려고 하다 죽어버린 황제도 많다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">단사</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">丹砂</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">상태의 수은이 피처럼 붉은 색을 띄고 있기 때문에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그것이 금을 녹여 넣는다는 신비성에서 이런 발상이 생겨났을 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다른 하나는 청산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">青酸</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청산은 과일의 씨앗이나 미성숙 과일에 약간씩 포함되어 있으므로 그것이 이용되었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">유명한 것은 복분자 비성숙 과일은 붉은 색이나 노란색</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원작의 세이가의 옷에 있는 연붉은 반점장</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">斑点状</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 모양은 복분자의 미성숙 과일이라고 생각된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시안화수소산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">은 금과 반응하여 시안화금</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(I)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 만든다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 물질은 시아노착체이기 때문에 물에 녹으며 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">([Au(Cn)2]), </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">실제로 청화금욕</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">青化金浴</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이라는 방법으로 금 도금에 사용된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이것으로 확실히 금은 녹으므로 복용할 수 있지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">당연히 청산가리 같이 위액</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">강산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">強酸</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">과 반응에 의해 독성이 강한 시안화수소</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">약산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">弱酸</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">을 발생시키기 때문에 맹독이 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">금의 성질과 상태</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아말감</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">착체</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">錯体</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">](</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">착이온</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">), </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">강산에 의한 약산유리반응</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">弱酸遊離反応</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">은 이과의 대학 수험에도 나오는 레벨이므로 잘 모르는 사람은 이과 사람에게 물어보자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요컨대 선단이라 하는 것은 기본적으로 독이었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세이가가 복분자를 다루고 있는 것을 생각하면 청산에 의한 외단술로 시해선이 되었을지도 모른다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">파랗기도 하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">靑 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">: </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">푸를 청</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청산에 의한 금액은 조금씩 복용하지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">위산도 나오지 낳는 극한의 공복상태</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그야말로 안개만 먹고 있는 상태</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에서 복용하면 이론상 독성은 나오지 않게 되긴 하지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">작품 내에서는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">선인이 된 나이는 겉모습의 연령이 멈췄다고 생각해</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">대체적으로 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">23~25</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세 정도의 모습이 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">말 그대로 목적을 위해 수단과 방법을 가리지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 과정에서 타인이 어떻게 되든 전혀 신경 쓰지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">품행방정 했던 남편인 곽 환은 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천살이 되기 전에 선인에서 천인으로 승화했지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세이가는 그 언동과 사념의 사악함에서 천인이 되지 못하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">본인도 될 생각이 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">애초에 천인은 항락의 반면제약이 많은데다 불멸이라고 할 수도 없고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천인오쇠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">), </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">덤으로 죽었을 때의 고통은 지옥보다 훨씬 심하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그렇기 때문에 불교에서는 육도윤회로부터 해탈을 추천하고 있지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역시 이쪽도 흥미가 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">성격이 나쁘다는걸 알고 있기 때문에 더욱 나쁘다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">욕이란 만물의 본질이면서 생명과 같으며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">악이랑 인간의 지혜이며 인간다움이라고 굳게 믿고 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다만 냉혹한 인간도 아니며 몰인정한 인간도 아니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">오히려 정이 너무 깊은 나머지 도착적인 성격으로 한 가지 일 이외에는 아무것도 보이지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그것이 주위에서 보기엔 각박하게 보인다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">강한 이의 곁에 있는 걸 좋아한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원래 일본에 온 것도 선인이 없기 때문에 효과적으로 그런 강자에게 어필할 수 있으리라는 노림수가 있었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">비녀 대신에 벽을 뚫는 끌은 남편이 남긴 것</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">결혼한 그 날 세이가는 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이런 도둑질 도구는 버려주세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">!</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 끌을 마루에 내던지며 말했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 두 사람 사이를 주선한 물건으로서 환은 버리려 하지 않고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">몸에서 떼지 않고 가지고 다녔다고 요재지이에 나와 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">12</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세 경에 세이가와 해후</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">邂逅</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도교의 가르침을 설명하며 이 때 세이가와 육체관계를 가진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어느 정도 배웠을 때 그 사념 때문에 세이가를 내쫓았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">설마 욕념을 읽히리라고는 예상도 못했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이대로 가면 안 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">목적을 이룰 수 없게 되어버린다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 세이가는 수를 썼다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">제일 안 되는 것은 거절당한 채 태자가 죽어서 끝나는 것</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그렇다 해서 멋대로 선인이 되어버려도 곁에는 있을 수 없게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어디까지나 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">선인이 되지 못하는 불쌍한 태자를 구원해주는 은인</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이라는 명목이 아니면 안 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그렇다면 그도 결코 거침없이 취급하지 못한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 태자와 헤어져 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">20</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 남짓 지날 때 쯤</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그녀는 어느 소녀와 맞닥뜨린다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">결국 만년</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">晩年</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 태자는 예상대로 다시 세이가에게 기대게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 때</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">누구든지 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명 더 선인이 될 수 있다고 수를 건다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">함께하든 실험대로 쓰든 마음대로 하라고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">30</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년간 계속해온 계획은 담담히 종착을 향해가고 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이미 여기까지 왔으면 어떤 희생이 생겨나도 상관없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아마 가장 소중하리라 생각되는 것은 이미 대가로서 지불해버렸으니까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여긴 다음 권에서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">!</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세이가의 계획</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요시카와의 관계</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">왜 토지코에게 집요하게 얽히려하는가</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/010.jpg"/></p>
<p></p>
<p class="moreless_fold" id="more2028_5"><span onclick="toggleMoreLess(this, '2028_5','미야코 요시카','접기'); return false;" style="cursor: pointer;">미야코 요시카</span></p>
<p></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/011.jpg"/></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사에서는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">膳部菩岐</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">々</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">美郎女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">](</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">젠노오오이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">膳大郎女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 쇼토쿠 태자의 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">3</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">번째 아내이며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가장 신뢰받으며 총애 받았던 인물이라고 일컫는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">호족 카시와데</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">膳</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가문의 출신</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카시와데노 오미카타부코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">膳臣傾子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 딸</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">상궁기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">上宮記</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 의하면 동생인 카시와데노히로코노이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">膳比里古郎女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 쇼토쿠 태자의 동생인 쿠메 황자의 아내가 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">598</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 쇼토쿠 태자와 결혼</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. 4</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">남 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">4</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">녀를 낳았고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">장녀인 츠키시네노 히메미코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">舂米女王</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자와 토지코노이라츠메의 장남인 야마시로노 오에 왕과 결혼했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 이루카에게 공격받았을 때</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">츠키시네노 히메미코는 야마시로노 오에 왕이나 태자들과 함께 자해를 했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">두 사람의 애정을 보여주는 에피소드로서 유명한 것은</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자가 그녀에게 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">죽을 때는 같이 묻힙시다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 말한 것</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 태자와 같은 시기에 병상에 누워</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자가 죽기 전날</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(622</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">4</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">월 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">7</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">) </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또는 같은 날에 죽은 것</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기서 태자는 정사</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">情死</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자살했다고 하는 견해가 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">) </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 말했던 대로 태자의 어머니</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">3</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명이서 예복사북고분</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">叡福寺北古墳</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 시나가노미사사기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">磯長陵</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 매장되었던 것 들 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그녀는 임종에 이르렀을 때 물을 원했지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자는 그것을 막고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">죽어가는 그녀를 보고있었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자는 죽은 애처에게 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">斑鳩</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">の </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">止美</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">の</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">井</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">の</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">水 生</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">かなくに </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">食</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">きてましもの </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">鳥見</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">の</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">井</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">の</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">水</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 노래를 읊었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">상궁성덕법왕제설</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자가 살고 있었다는 것으로 유명한 이카루가의 땅은 카시와데 가문의 본거지이며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">권력을 점점 강화시키는 소가 가문의 영향에서 떨어져있기 때문에 아내가 있는 곳으로 몸을 두었다고도 일컫는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자가 현재 법륭사동원가람</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">法隆寺東院伽藍</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">근처에 있던 이카루가 궁으로 이사한 것은 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">605</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">당시는 남편이 아내에게 찾아가는 왕래혼이기도 했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세리츠미히메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">芹摘姫</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 전승</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">병상에 누워있는 어머니를 위해 들에서 미나리를 따는 소녀와 카시와데 가문의 영지에서 만난 태자는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 모습에 반해 그 아가씨를 아내로 맞는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 아가씨가 바로 카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메 였다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아니면 이 아가씨가 카시와데 가문의 양녀가 되어 카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메로서 결혼했다고도 전해진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다만 이건 유랴쿠 천황</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">雄略天皇</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 설화의 패러디일지도 모른다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 지역에는 카시와데데라</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">膳夫寺</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메가 어머니의 보리</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">菩提</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 애도하기 위해 건립한 절이 남아있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미야코노이라츠메는 천손본기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">天孫本紀</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에만 쓰여 있는 모노노베 가문의 여성</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베노 모리야의 배다른 동생인 모노노베노 니에코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">物部贄子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 딸이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천손본기에서 니에코는 배다른 동생인 후츠히메와 결혼해있지만 그 자식에 미야코노이라츠메는 명기되어있지 않고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또한 후츠히메 이외의 니에코의 아내는 일절불명이며 미야코노이라츠메의 어머니는 누구인지 알 수 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미야코노이라츠메는 아버지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어머니</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">?)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 형</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">즉 모노노베노 모리야의 형</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">인 모노노베노 미카리</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">物部御狩</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">와 결혼하여 두 아이를 낳는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사실 방금 기술과 이것밖에 쓰여 있지 않다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미야코노요시카</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">都良香</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 쇼토쿠 태자의 시대보다 나중</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">헤이안 시대의 문인이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">한시에 뛰어나고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스가와라노 미치자네</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">菅原道真</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가 대책</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">관리의 등용시험</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">을 수험했을 때 문답 박사를 맡은 것으로 유명</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">굉장히 강한 육체를 가지고 있었지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">궁핍한 생활이었다고도 일컫는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일본삼대실록</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">日本三代実録</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스기와라노 미치자네</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">菅原道真</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에게 관직으로 추월당해 실망하고 오오미네 산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">大峯山</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 올라</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 후</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">100</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 뒤 젊은 모습으로 요시카가 나타났다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">본조신선전</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">本朝神仙伝</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미야코노요시카는 미치자네와 대항하는 에피소드에 등장한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그런 미치자네는 다이고 천황</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">碮醐天皇</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 황위의 찬탈을 꾸몄다는 오명을 쓰고 좌천되어 다자이후</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">太宰府</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에서 죽는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 후 다이고 천황의 자손이 연달아 병사해</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청량전</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">清涼殿</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 떨어진 낙뢰로 조정의 요인이 다수 사상하여</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 번개를 본 다이고 천황도 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">3</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">개월 후 붕어</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;
