letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">뇌신이 된 미치자네의 원령이라고 두려움 받아</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">죽은 뒤에 죄가 면해져 증위되었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">더불어 천신님으로서 신앙 받아 괴이는 되지 않았다고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">나성문</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">羅城門</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에서 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">気霽</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">れては</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">風新柳</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">の</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">髪</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">を</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">梳</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">る</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 노래를 읊은 것을 이바라키 동자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">茨木童子</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">로 여겨지는 오니가 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">氷消</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">えては</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">波旧苔</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">の</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">鬚</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">を</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">洗</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">ふ</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 대답</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">십훈초</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">十訓抄</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이바라카센 제 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">화에서 카센이 읊은 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">水消</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">えて </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">波</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">を </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">旧苔</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">の</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">髪</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">を</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">洗</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">う</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 이걸 살짝 바꾼 거라고 생각된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">본조신선전에서는 어떤 사람이 미야코노요시카의 노래를 읊었을 때</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">주작문</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">朱雀門</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 있던 오니가 감탄했다고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">삼천세계는 눈앞에 다하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">십이인연은 마음 속을 비우니</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. [</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">三千世界</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">は</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">眼前</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">に</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">尽</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">き</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">。</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">十二因縁</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">は</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">心裏</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">に</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">空</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">し</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">。</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 넷째 구는 벤자이텐</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">弁財天</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 미야코노요시카에게 가르쳐준 거라고도 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">강담초</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">江談抄</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 시는 신선전</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">神仙伝</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">], </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">열선전</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">列仙伝</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">등에서 인용한 것이 많다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기에서도 선계에 대한 동경이 보인다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">강시는 혼백 가운데 혼을 잃고 움직이는 시체</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">강시</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">僵尸</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 글자는 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">경직된 시체</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 의미</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사람은 정신을 지탱하는 기의 삼혼</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천혼</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">天魂</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">지혼</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">地魂</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">인혼</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">人魂</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">])</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">과 육체를 지탱하는 기의 칠백</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">기쁨</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">분노</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">슬픔</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">두려운</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사랑</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">악함</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">욕망</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">으로 이루어진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">혼은 하늘로 돌아가고 백은 땅으로 돌아간다고 하지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">정확하게는 올바르게 매장되지 않거나 깊은 원념에 싸인 채 죽은 자가 혼만을 잃고 백으로 움직이는 강시가 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또한</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도사가 집을 떠난 사람의 시체를 고향까지 돌려보내기 위해 멋대로 걷는 강시를 만드는 경우도 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">작품 내에서는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자의 아내</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">膳部菩岐</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">々</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">美郎女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 만화로 만드는데 이름이 너무 긴 것과 젠노오오이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">膳大郎女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 것도 분위기와 달랐기 때문에 카시와데노미노이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">膳美郎女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">로 했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자의 애칭은 미노이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">美郎女</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">만화</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">해 뜨는 곳의 천자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 동일인물에 해당되는 카시와데노미노이라츠메를 모방한 것이기도 하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">지적장애자인 것도 공통</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">결혼의 시기는 토지코와 똑같이</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">전개상 무시했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">작품 내에서는 태자가 미노이라츠메라고 부르는건</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">결혼한 당초</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">본명인 카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메를 그녀 자신이 기억하지 못하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미노이라츠메만을 기억해서 그걸로 정착 되버렸다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원작 안에 있어서 요시카는 종교전쟁을 잘 기억하지 못하지만 경험한 듯한 말투로 이야기하기 때문에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시대적으로 미야코노요시카보다 미야코노이라츠메 쪽이 적당하다고 생각했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원작에서는 요시카의 눈은 까만색에서 회색으로 후토와 같다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토 쪽이 약간 밝다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">) </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코는 거의 황색의 느낌이 나고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코는 미코와 눈동자 색을 밝게 한 느낌이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">매일 멍하게 상기된 듯한 표정으로 살고 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자가 읽은 한시를 읊으면 태자가 기뻐하므로 조금씩 외우고 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">말할 필요도 없이 여기서 읊는 시는 모두 미야코노요시카가 만든 한시</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">헤이안 시대</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세이가가 미야코노요시카로서 관직에 오르게 해</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">기억에 남겨진 태자와의 추억의 시를 읊은 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">본래는 미야코노이라츠메라는 이름을 가졌지만 태자는 모른다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원래 모노노베 가문의 딸이었던 그녀는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">호족인 카시와데 가문의 양녀가 되어 태자와 만났다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자의 각별한 총애를 받고 있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코보다도 곁에 있는 시간이 길다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">육체적인 관계도 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">4</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명의 아내 가운데 제일 강하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토의 말에 따르면 체취인지 물들인 향기인지 알 수 없지만 신기한 향기가 난다는 것</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">악취는 아니지만 너무 강해서 거북하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">옆에 있기만 하는 인간에게도 옮을 정도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이건 아까 말한 태자와 죽고 소생한 기인의 향기의 일화를 소재로 삼았고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또한 요시카</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">芳香</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 이름을 나타내는 것으로 삼고 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">살아있을 적이므로 시체의 냄새를 없애기 위한 것은 아니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">기인의 향기로운</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">芳</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">しい</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">] </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">냄새</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">香</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">り</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 것을 생각하면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">당시의 세이가 냥냥도 역시 같은 향기를 내고 있던 것이 되는데</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">주변 시중은 최저한밖에 하지 못하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 이상한 정신상태도 있어서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">남 앞에 나서는 일은 없으며 태자와 단 둘의 세계에서 살고 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세이가의 손으로 요시카라고 이름 지어져 강시가 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다만 세이가와는 이전부터 관계가 있었고 살아있을 적에도 이상한 거동을 보인다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">작중의 두 사람의 대화</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사적으로도 쇼토쿠 태자가 말한 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">죽을 때는 같이 묻힙시다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 대답은 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">멋진 무덤에 묻히죠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">즉 신령묘 </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">3</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">면의 도중 음악명</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 토지코는 말하지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 또 다른 주인공</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이건 그녀의 복수의 이야기이기도 하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여긴 다음 권에서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">!</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세이가와의 관계성</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그녀의 복수란</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">강시가 된 그녀의 차후</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/012.jpg"/></p>
<p></p>
<p class="moreless_fold" id="more2028_6"><span onclick="toggleMoreLess(this, '2028_6','인물상관도','접기'); return false;" style="cursor: pointer;">인물상관도</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/013.jpg"/></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">560</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 이전</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">무 청아 탄생</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">혼인하여 곽 청아가 되고 시해선으로</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">560</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년경</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토히메 탄생</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">570</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년경</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토히메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이소노카미 신궁의 사이구가 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">572</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">예부터 야마토 왕권에 직속해온 씨족을 무라지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">連</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라 하고 모노노베 가문</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">오오토모 가문</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">나카토미 가문 등을 예로 들 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">야마토 왕권에 복속한 기내</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">畿内</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">주변의 유력 호족을 오미</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">臣</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 하고 소가 가문</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가츠라기 가문</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아베 가문 등을 예로 들 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">당시 국정은 천황 아래에서 무라지의 최고 권력자 오오무라지와 오미의 최고 권력자 오오오미가 관리하고 있었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 이래</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">종교적으로 상반되는 소가 가문과 모노노베 가문의 싸움</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">즉 숭불파</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">VS</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">폐불파의 싸움은 점점 격화된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">574</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">585</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년경</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카쿠 세이가 일본 방문</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토요사토미미노 미코에게 도교를 전하려 하지만 사선이라는게 알려져 거절당한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">585</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토요사토미미노 미코의 아버지</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요메이 천황 즉위</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">587</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요메이 천황 붕어</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역병에 의한 죽음</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 직전에 모노노베 가문에 의한 대대적인 폐불이 있었기 때문에 비난의 화살은 모노노베 가문에게 향한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">종교전쟁</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토히메의 오라비</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베노 모리야 전사</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베 가문의 몰락과 소가 가문의 융성</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">잔존한 모노노베 가문은 이후</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사이구이며 모리야의 동생인 후토히메를 따르게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 후는 눈에 띄지 않았지만 소가 가문과의 작은 싸움이 멈추지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 우마코의 추천으로 스슌 천황 즉위</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">592</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스슌 천황</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 우마코에게 시살</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">593</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스이코 천황 즉위</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토요사토미미노 미코는 섭정이 되어 소가 가문과 함께 절대적인 권력을 가진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">595</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년경</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토요사토미미노 미코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스이코 천황의 딸인 우지노카이타코노히메미코와 결혼</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">얼마 지나지 않아 우지노카이타코노히메미코 사망</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">600</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년경</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">610</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년경</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토히메가 환속</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사이구를 그만두는 것</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">),</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 우마코에게 시집을 가 토지코의 어머니가 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이것으로 모노노베 가문과 소가 가문 사이의 평화를 굳히게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토요사토미미노 미코가 토지코노이라츠메와의 약혼을 비밀리에 소가노 우마코와 결정한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코노이라츠메와 카시와데노미노이라츠메가 토요사토미미노 미코와 혼인</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이후 순서대로</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">3</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">남</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">녀</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">· 4</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">남</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">4</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">녀를 낳는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토요사토미미노 미코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카시와데노미노이라츠메가 사는 이카루가 궁에 거점을 둔다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">615</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년경</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이후</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">남</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">녀를 낳는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">620</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년경</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box; text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">622</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">같은 날 토지코노이라츠메 사망</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시해선의 술법은 실패</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">같은 날 후토히메 사망</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">4</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">월</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">8</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일 토요사토미미노 미코 사망</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">628</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스이코 천황 붕어</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">629</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토요사토미미노 미코와 토지코노이라츠메의 제</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">황자</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">야마시로노 오에 왕</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">황위를 다투지만 져서 조메이 천황</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다무라 황자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">즉위</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">643</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 이루카</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이카루가 궁을 공격</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">야마시로노 오에 왕</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아내인 츠키시네노오오키미</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자와 카시와데노미노이라츠메의 딸</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">과 함께 자해</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자의 혈통인 상궁왕가 절단</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">645</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 이루카</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에미시</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">나카노오오에 황자들에 의해 을사의 변으로 사망</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가 가문의 몰락</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다음날에 나카노 오에 황자가 다이카 개신을 발령</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box; text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p style="box-sizing: border-box; text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">＿人人 人人＿</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">＞ 대부활 ＜</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">￣Y^Y^Y^Y￣</span></p>
<p><br/></p>
<p class="moreless_fold" id="more2028_7"><span onclick="toggleMoreLess(this, '2028_7','신령묘 창작 추천 원전 소개','접기'); return false;" style="cursor: pointer;">신령묘 창작 추천 원전 소개</span></p>
<p><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><br/></span></p>
<p><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><br/></span></p>
<p><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;">●</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box;">고사기</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;">古事記</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일본에서 제일 오래된 역사서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">히에다노 아레가 암송하고 있던 천황의 계보나 전승을 써서 남긴 것이라고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천지의 시작부터 스이코 천황의 붕어까지를 기록해놓았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일본의 신화</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">전설의 상당수는 여기에 쓰여 있다고 해도 과언이 아니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">신의 계통부터 그 지배의 정당성을 이야기하는 뉘앙스</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">처음부터 천상에 타카마가하라</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">高天原</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가 있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 주인인 아마테라스 오오미카미</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">天照大神</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 계보가 세상을 다스려야 한다고 그려진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">지상의 주권도 당연히 천상에 있는 거라고 여겨진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가요가 많이 삽입되어있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가장 오래된 와카라고 여겨지는</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">팔운이 솓는 이즈모 팔중담</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">처와 삶의 팔중담을 만드니</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 팔중담을</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">八雲</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">たつ</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">八雲八 重垣妻</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">ごみに</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">八重圾作</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">るその</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">八重垣</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">を</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도 수록되어있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일본서기는 조정의 아래에서 만들어져 공개되었기 때문에 개찬이 많았다고 여겨지지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 점에서 정사가 아닌 고사기는 비교적 원재료에 따른 것이라고 생각할 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일본서기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">日本書紀</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일본에서 가장 오래된 정사</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">正史</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">],</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">즉 조정이 스스로 편찬한 공식 역사서다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">올바른 역사의 의미가 아니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천지개벽부터 지토 천황의 시대까지를 기록해놓았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도네리 친왕</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">舎人親王</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 짓고 모아진 것</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">고사기와 같이 많은 신화 전설이 쓰여 있지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이상한 기술이 쓰인 부분도 많다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">중국의 사서의 영향을 강하게 받은 것이라 생각되고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천황 신화이면서도 고사기에 비해 국가의 동란에 초점이 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">타카마가하라나 황천</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">黄泉</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">은 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">지상계와 천상계는 대등하게 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이쪽은 고사기처럼 예정조화적이지 않고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">무력에 의해 나라를 통치하는 것이 변천한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">본래는 이것보다 전에 쇼토쿠 태자가 정리된 역사서</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">국기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">国記</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천황기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">天皇記</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가 있었지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 에미시가 저택에 불을 질렀을 때 불타버렸다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 이루카를 암살하고 소가 가문을 멸망시킨 텐지 천황에게 좋지 못한 역사서였기 때문에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자신의 정당성을 유지하기 위해 처분하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">정사로 역사를 덧썼다는 설도 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">상궁성덕법왕제설</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">上宮聖德法王帝說</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자의 불교적 실적을 주로 쓴 전기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에도 시대 말기까지 호류지에 수납되어 있던 것으로 천하의 고본이라고 여겨진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">내용도 고사기나 일본서기 이전의 자료가 근본이 되어있다고 여겨져 신용성은 제법 높다고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">선대구사본기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">先代旧事本紀</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span></p>
