<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천지개벽부터 스이코 천황까지를 기록한 역사서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 다른 역사서를 모아붙인 것으로 위서로 인정받았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">말하자면 천하의 복붙책</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 일부 독자적인 기술이 있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">니기하야히노미코토의 기술이 이상하게 많은 점에서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">현존하지 않는 모노노베 가문의 자료를 인용한 것이 아니냐는 것으로 가치를 가진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">짓궂게도 이 복붙성 때문에 가치가 생기지 않는다고 해야 할까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">독자의 기술은</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">3, 5, 10</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">권</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 책에서는</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">5</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">권의 천손본기를 많이 가져왔다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미야코노이라츠메의 기술이 있는 것은 이 문헌뿐</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토히메는 배다른 오라비인 모노노베노 니에코와 결혼하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미야코노이라츠메는 니에코의 딸이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">부상략기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">扶桑略記</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">헤이안 시대의 사찬 역사서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">진무 천황부터 호리카와 천황이 다스리는 시대까지를 써</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교 관련의 기사를 중심으로 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자나 소가 가문에 관련된 기술도 많다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">상궁성덕태자전보궐기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">上宮聖徳太子伝補闕記</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">조사</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">調使</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">],</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카시와데노 오미의 집안 기록을 기본으로 쓰인 쇼토쿠 태자의 전기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">신선담적인 사건의 기술이 많다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천수국수장</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">天寿國繍帳</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자의</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">4</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">번째 아내인 타치바나노오오이라츠메가 태자의 죽음을 안타까워하며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천수국</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">극락정토</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 있는 태자의 모습을 보고 싶다는 생각으로 만든 만다라</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">옷에 자수가 있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">제작의 경위가 문자로 쓰여 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">世間</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">は</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">虚假</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">にして</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">、</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">ただ</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">仏</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">のみこれ</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">裒</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">なり</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 태자의 유언도 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">성덕태자전력</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">聖徳太子伝暦</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아나호베노하시히토노히메미코가 쇼토쿠 태자를 임신했을 때부터</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가 가문의 멸망까지를 기록한 쇼토쿠 태자의 전설</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">거의</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">살마다 태자에게 일어난 이상한 일화가 소개된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기서는 무려</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">11</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">살 경</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">인솔하고 있던</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">36</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명의 아이의 이야기를 동시에 들었다고 적혀있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">●</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요재지이</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">聊齋志異</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청아</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 항목이 있는 중국의 신선담</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">술벌레 등의 이야기도 수록되어있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사서는 아니지만 읽을거리로서는 재밌다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이것들은</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">web</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">상에 원문</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">주석</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">재해석</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">현대어 번역이 올라와 있는 것도 많으므로 부담 없이 접할 수 있습니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="moreless_fold" id="more2028_8"><span onclick="toggleMoreLess(this, '2028_8','신령묘 2차 창작 포인트','접기'); return false;" style="cursor: pointer;">신령묘 2차 창작 포인트</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"><br/></span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"><br/></span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 토지코</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">애초에 왜 여기 있어</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">?</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 곳부터 의문이 생긴다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자의 수반으로서 후토는 설정 상 이해할 수 있지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코의 입장은 굉장히 어중간하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">왜냐하면 역사 자료에서는 압도적으로 쇼토쿠 태자와 카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메의 부부애가 쓰여 있는데 반해</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코노이라츠메는 명백하게 그저 정략결혼이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코와 태자의 에피소드는 너무 적고 제</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">황자를 낳았긴 했지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가 가문의 딸이라 말할 것도 없는 불교도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">신토와 궁합이나 도교와의 친화성도 나쁘다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">더불어 애처로 취급받는 카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메는 태자가 죽기 전날 또는 당일에 죽었다는 점에서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시해술과의 관련도 의심해보고 싶은 좋은 상황이 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코가 시해선의 술법을</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">실패했다고는 해도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">받았다는 것을 생각해보면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코가 있는데도 호키키미노이라츠메가 없는 것은 한 층 더 이상하다고 할 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코라는 이름도 굳이 도륙한다의 도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">屠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 글자를 쓴 거라면 어떤 의미를 붙여보고 싶은 상황</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원령이라는 성질상 심하게 무언가 원망하는 사건이 있었다는 것은 쉽게 상상되므로</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기도</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">차창작의 실력을 보여줄 곳</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">신주는 인터뷰에서 토지코노이라츠메와 토지코는 동일인물이 아니라고 부정했고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">중</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">병 같은 이름을 붙였다고 말했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">주변에서는 모처럼 역사대로의 두 사람의 관계에 물을 끼얹는 거라고 조금 물의를 빚고 있었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 미코토지를 좋아한다면 그런 섣불리 결론지을 정도는 아니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">ㅡㅡ『……</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그러니까 모노노베 가문이 보스로 정해져 있었어요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">보너스 적으로 소가 가문의 토지코가 나오면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또 의외성이 있을 거라고 생각해서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">ㅡㅡ『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그런 보너스였습니까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일단은 쇼토쿠 태자의 아내라는 것이지요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">?</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">ㅡㅡ『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일단은 말이죠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">ㅡㅡ『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 환상향에 오니까 양쪽 다 여자인데요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……』</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">ㅡㅡ『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그건 이름이 닮았을 뿐이고 다른 사람이니까요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자신을 도륙한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">自分</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">を</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">屠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">る</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 엄청난 중</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">병 같은 이름으로 말이죠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">캬라</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">☆</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">멜</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">febri vol.09 p.58</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">신령묘 인터뷰에서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 부분에 대해서 의외로 해석도 곡해도 가능한 것을 알게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">우선</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일단 쇼토쿠 태자의 아내</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 대해서는 애초에 부정이 되지 않았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">오히려 적극적으로 부부 관계라는 점으로</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이른바 일반적인 부부의 형태가 아니라고 해도</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일단</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">무언가의 관계가 있다고 읽어 들이는 게 자연스럽지 않을까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">보너스 적으로 소가 가문의 토지코를 내보면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">~</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 순수하게 역사 인물을 가리키는 토지코를 이름만 바꿨다는 가능성도 있지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">문헌적으로 확실히 아내라고 여겨지는 토지코노이라츠메를 자작 게임의 캐릭터로 만들어 설정을 만들 정도로 잘 알고 있는 신주가</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일단은 말이죠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 함축을 돌려보내는 것은 약간 부자연스러움</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">극단적으로 말하면 여기서</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자의 아내로서의 토지코노이라츠메</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">=</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 부정당했지만</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자와 토지코의 부부적인 관계</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">에 대해서는 오히려 거의 긍정되고 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자는 애초에 정식 혼인 상대만으로</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">4</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명이 있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 외에 관계를 가진 인간도 생각할 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">부부적인 관계라는 것도 혼인 없는 남녀관계나</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">남녀관계 없는 혼인</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사실혼 등 여러 가지가 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 부근은 미코의 생전의 성별에 관계될 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">더 말하자면</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이름이 닮았을 뿐으로 다른 사람</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">은 미코에게도 적용할 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코는 정확히는 쇼토쿠 태자라고 하기보다</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">태자 신앙에서 형성된 우상</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이라고 하는 편이 올바르다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그렇기에 최종 스펠</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">갓 태어난 신령</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세로 이동만으로 대체적으로 어떻게 된다는 둥 시구식 같은 말은 하지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사실 대부분의 동방 캐릭터가</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">전승적으로 오리지널의 일화를 가지는 인물이 바깥 세계에서 풍화되어</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 이미지만으로 형성된 다른 사람이 환상향에 태어난다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 가능성도 높다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그러자면 뭐 확실히 토지코도 미코도 다른 사람이 되어버리지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">두 사람의 부부 관계는 전승에 있으니까 그걸 오리지널로서 파생시킨 상사부하 관계라는 것이 타당하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다른 사람이든 아니든 토지코와 쇼토쿠 태자의 관계성은 잔류하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">캐릭터로서도 부부관계가 무언가의 밑거름이 되어있다고 고찰하는 건 그렇게 부자연스럽지 않을 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코토지는 역사상 사실</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">은 미묘하지만</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">우마야도 황자</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">×</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코노이라츠메는 역사상 사실</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">은 대체적으로 정답이고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기서는 멋대로 만든</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코토지는 전설</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">을 짐작해본다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">허구의 뉘앙스를 곁들여서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">신주의 현실의 말까지 자세히 고찰하는 건 좀 그렇지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 부분을 적당히 흘려 넘기려고 말한 것으로 해버리면 인터뷰 그 자체가 의미를 잃어버리게 되므로 용서해주시길</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">탈선했지만 게임이나 설정집의 서적이 아니기 때문에 이걸 공식설정이라고 하는 것도 약간 미묘한 부분이고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어찌됐든</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">차 창작 내에서는 자기책임으로 마음대로 해석해도 되는 부분이기도 하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">순수하게 부부로 삼는 것도 좋고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">부부 관계의 전승에서 파생된 새로운 관계성을 창조하는 것도 좋다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">말할 것도 없지만 원 소재에 있어서 역사상 사실의 부부관계에서 완전히 떨어진 친구나 주종 관계로 두 사람을 이야기 하는 것도 마찬가지로 좋은 생각이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">굳이 신주가 말하는 것에 충실하게 따르면서 두 사람의 친애를 다루는 것도 제법 재밌다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">예를 들면 카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메 야말로 지금의 토지코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">≠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">과거 토지코</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라던지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또는 그녀를 궁녀나 시중인과 같은 부하</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가신이나 친구로서 다루는 것도 좋을 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 어떤 이유로 시해선이 되었어야 할 카시와데노호키키미노이라츠메와 뒤바뀌는 것도 좋다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스스로 과거를 도륙하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">과거를 도륙하여 나는 소생한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. [</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">自</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">らを</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">古</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">に</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">屠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">る</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">、</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">古</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">に</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">屠</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">りて</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">我蘇</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">る</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">],</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 할 것 같은 이름은 과거의 말살을 느끼게 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그럼 굳이 토지코노이라츠메와 다른 입장을 갖게 했을 때에 친화성도 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">제물로 바쳐진 아이라는 이름으로 해도 좋다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">예를 들면 우마코와 천민의 아이였다던가</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">근친상간의 아이였다던가</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코노이라츠메의 그림자 무사나 미움 받는 쌍둥이라는 식으로도 손대본다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">차라리 토지코노이라츠메 쪽이 양녀고 토지코가 친자식이라는 것도 좋다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 토지코는 어떤 이유로 태자의 아내가 되지 못하고 양녀인 토지코가 친 자식으로서 태자와 이어졌다든지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토의 에피소드에서 살짝 손댔지만 카와카미노이라츠메와 토지코를 동일시하여 스슌 천황의 전 신부로서 그것도 천황의 암살범과 내통하고 있었다는 설정도 가능하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카와카미노이라츠메는 스슌 천황이 암살당한 후</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">암살범인 야마토노아야노 코마에게 강제로 아내로 삼아진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">코마는 우마코에게 처형당하고 카와카미노이라츠메는 역사에서 모습을 감춘다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그렇기 때문에 이름을 바꿨다는 것으로 해도 좋다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이렇게 하면 스슌 천황의 아내로서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토와 같은 남편을 가진 인간으로 삼는 것도 불가능은 아니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 그 후물림이 태자에게 왔다고 생각하면 질척질척해져 그런 것도 아주 좋다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사를 무시해도 방법은 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. 1400</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년간 토지코는 혼자였다고 생각된다</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자고 있었을지도 모르지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">).</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">인간도</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">10</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">20</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 지나면 성격 같은 건 변해버릴 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그저 혼뿐인 존재인 토지코는</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1400</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 동안에 얼마나 변해버린 것일까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이미 원래 토지코의 인격이라는 것조차 닳아 풍화되어버렸을지도 모른다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기부터 약간 억지지만 다른 사람이라는 것도 말 못할 건 없지 않을까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">억지지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 육체가 없는 그녀는 정신적인 큰 변혁 그 자체로 다른 사람이라고 할 수 있을 포텐셜을 가진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1400</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 동안 조금씩 미쳐가 그 모습은 인간이라기보다 무서운 악귀나 요수와 같은 모습으로 변해버렸고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 재회해서 다시 사람으로 돌아올 수 있었다던가 그런 이야기도 보고 싶다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">영체의 다리를 그 자취로 해도 좋을지도 모른다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자연스럽게 그 다리라는 것도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">제법 해석하는 방법에 따라서는 맛있게 조리할 수 있을 거 같다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">설정이 적은데도 원 소재의 캐릭터로서는 생각보다 핵심적인 그녀이기 때문에 창작에서는 최대한 활용해보자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자와 그 아내의 에피소드는 어쩐지 재미있는 소재가 널려있기 때문에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기를 통째로 놓치는 것은 아내의 이름을 쓴 이상 좀 아깝다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">물론 그런 귀찮은 일 할 필요 없이 토지코노이라츠메</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">=</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코로서 원래 부부가 러브러브 쪽쪽하는 것도 굉장히 좋다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코토지 섹스 주세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">みことじセックス</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">ください</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토요사토미미노 미코</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">생각보다 소재로는 어려움이 느껴지지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그것보다 쇼토쿠 태자의 일화는 정말 대량으로 있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원전부터 시작해 전혀 자중하지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 책도 쇼토쿠 태자의 일화는 유명한 곳 이외에 그렇게까지 건드리지 않았다고 할지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">제대로 전부 써서 고찰하면 이 책이</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">10</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">권이 있어도 모자란다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">것보다 인쇄비로 죽는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어릴 적에도 자주 들은 좋은 냄새로 둘러싸인 쇼토쿠 태자라면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시해선으로서 소녀의 몸으로 다시 태어났을 때 엄청 소녀취가 났음이 틀림없을 거다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">!</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라던가 뭐든지 가능하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 소재가 너무 많아 반대로 어디부터 시작하면 좋을지 모르겠다면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">완전히 다른 방향에서 가져와도 좋은</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">key person</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">뱌쿠렌이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">뱌쿠렌은 구문구수에서 미코와 카나코와 함께 왁자지껄 화기애애하게 이야기하고 있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">경우에 따라서는 뱌쿠렌과 미코는 싸울지 화해할지가 생겨날 것 같은 상황이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사적으로도 소재는 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">뱌쿠렌이 있었던 절은 시기산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">信貴山</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 조고손시사</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">朝護孫子寺</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 일컫는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 조고손시사의 개조</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">開祖</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 쇼토쿠 태자라고 전해진다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">종교전쟁도 마지막의 모리야 토벌 즈음에 쇼토쿠 태자는 사천왕의 상을 조각한</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">인의 년</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">인의 날</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">인의 각에 비사문천이 머리맡에서 서있었고 그 가호로 모리야를 이겼다는 등의 설화가 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쇼토쿠 태자는 그것 때문에</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">594</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">년 비사문천을 모시는 절을 세우고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 절이 있는 산을 시기산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">信貴山</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">](</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">믿고 존경해야할 산</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이라고 이름 지었다고 한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">비사문천과 호랑이를 모시는 것도 이 때문</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 토요사토미미노 미코는 불교를</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아마도 뱌쿠렌보다 훨씬</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자세히 알고 있을 거라고 생각되는데</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교를 도구로서 사용해 도교에 매진했다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코가 불교를 소홀히 하는 행위는 들켜있고 뱌쿠렌이 그것을 알고 있었다고 해도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">적어도 알았을 당초에는 쇼크였을 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">왜냐하면 쇼토쿠 태자는 불교의 카리스마로서 존경받는 우상이며</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">자신 그리고 나아가서는 동생의 절의 개조</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">開祖</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이며 본래는 외경해야 하는 인물이기 때문에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이렇게 하면 언뜻 보기엔 양쪽은 완전히 다른 사람이라는 생각을 가지게 되지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 현재에 이르러 사상은</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">죽음에 대한 공포</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 완전히 같은 것이었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코는 활로를 다른 종교인 도교를 통해 인간을 넘는 것으로 달성했고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">뱌쿠렌은 불교도이면서도 사도적</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">邪道的</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;
