letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">으로 인간을 버리는 방향으로 길을 벗어났다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사실은 지나온 길도 똑같은 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교는 기도해도 아무것도 해주지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라는 저류</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">底流</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가 양쪽 모두에게 흐르고 있다고 해도 어쩔 수 없으리</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">두 사람은 어디까지나 서로 화합할 수도 있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어디까지나 서로 틀어질 수 있는 매력적인 관계라고 말할 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 명련사</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">수수한 문지기인 쿄코가 미코의 천적이 될 것 같아 그건 그거대로 재밌다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">전개상</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">보스 같은 상대에게 당하는 최종 보스의 그림은 판타지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">물론</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원래 아내로서의 토지코와의 관계도 신경 쓰이고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">두 사람의 앞날도 보고 싶다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코토지 섹스 주세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">みことじセックスください</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">].</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베노 후토</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사 내에서는 아까 말했듯이 궁극의 악녀</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">&amp;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">트러블 메이커인 트릭스터다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사랑하는 사이가 됐을 남자도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 우마코</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베노 니에코</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스슌 천황과 문헌을 뒤져보면 이렇게까지 하는 건가 싶을 정도로 엄청난 것도 다수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아마 더 있으리라</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하는 짓도 지독하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">게다가 종교전쟁의 종결에 관련된 모리야의 동생이라는 입장은 굉장히 맛있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">오라비를 죽이게 되는 심경을 상상할수록 이야기의 깊이가 나온다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">유효하게 활용하고 싶은 설정은 역시</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">토지코와의 혈연관계 또는 미코와의 의붓 장모 관계일 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">연령과 분위기 적인 문제는 있지만 드문 어머니 캐릭터다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어머니 나름의 애정을 털어놓는 것도 좋고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어머니의 참견으로 두 사람을 안달복달 시키는 것도 좋고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">글러먹은 어머니 진상을 부려도 좋고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코와 배덕적인 관계를 쌓는 것도 좋다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가족 관계</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">혈연관계가 제법 명확한 것은 신령묘의 특징이기도 하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">풍신록은 자손 선조지만 조금 시대가 떨어져있어 가족이라기보다 일족이라는 느낌</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코와 토지코 양쪽 모두 중개하는 것도 가능하고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어느 한쪽과 특별한 관계를 가진다는 것도 이상하지 않다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">연령적인 문제는 계모나 선술 같은 것으로 해결할 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">남편과 아내의 장모라는 삼자관계는 여러모로 장난칠 수 있는 게 있으므로 적극적으로 사용하고 싶다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아내와 남편의 사이를 방해하는 장모도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">애처가 남편에게 엄하게 대하는 장모도 좋은 흐름이면서 나쁘지 않다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">실제로 피가 이어졌다는 설정은 크다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이와후네도 역시 여러모로 써먹을 만 하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">성동녀라는 것에서 일부러 혈연을 끊고 처녀성을 주장하는 것도 작은 즐거움</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">거기서 더해 후토는 모노노베 가문으로서 폐불이나 사원의 방화에 가담해왔다고 생각할 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기서 또 명련사다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">명련사에 트집을 잡는 것도 전혀 이상하지 않고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">불교를 싫어하고 있는 설정에서 장난을 걸어도 재밌다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또 니기하야히노미코토나 타케미카즈치 강림의 이와후네와 관련되거나</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">쿠니유즈리 신화를 인용해서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모리야 신사와의 인연을 만드는 것도 좋다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카나코의 천적 틱하게</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">표면상 불교측에 가담한 것을 기억하고 있다면 꿍꿍이가 있다고 생각해야 할 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">바보 설정과 책사 설정을 교묘하게 혼합시키는 시키는 것도 캐릭터 매력의 하나</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여담이지만 푸딩을 먹고 있는 모습이 어울리는 것은 오쟈루마루의 영향인가</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카쿠 세이가</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">굉장히 편리</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하다는 것도 세이가에 한해서는 사방팔방 원전을 찾을 필요가 없고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요재지이</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">권으로 거의 충분하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이와나미 쇼텐 요재지이</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">를 추천</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원 소재도 그 안에서 완결되어있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">밤에 몰래 숨어드는 것에 실패한 소년과 부부가 되지만 어느 날 죽어버리고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">사실은 시해선이 되었다고 하는 이야기</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사적으로는 쇼토쿠 태자보다 나중의 이야기지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 시대의 엇갈림을 소재를 중심으로 집어넣는 건 조금 생각해볼 필요가 있을 것 같다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">타임 슬립이 가능하다고 생각하면 너무 마음대로 되어버려서 그냥 사기 캐릭이 될 수도 있기 때문에 여기는 섬세하게 취급하고 싶다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">비교적 최근 바깥의 세계에 왕래할 수 있는 듯한 묘사도 있으므로</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">산타 라던지</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하쿠레이 대결계는 구멍으로 빠져나갈 수 있을지도 모른다고 고찰하면 또 여러모로 떠오를 것 같다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원전대로라면 시시하다고 생각하는 사람은 오히려 반기를 들어보면 어떨까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 요재지이의</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청아</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">는 찔러볼 곳이 많다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">결혼 같은 건 절대로 하지 않겠다고 결의한 청아가</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">최종적인 부모의 권유라는 것을 가미해도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">밤에 몰래 숨어든 날을 경계로 그렇게 간단하게 결혼하고 출산하는 흐름이 될까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">?</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 부분은 원전에 있어서도 완전히 당돌하게 청아가 변심하고 있어 당돌한 부분이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">곽 한은 둘째 치고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그 날부터 청아까지 결혼에 긍정적으로 되어버린다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">애초에 곽 한의 밤에 몰래 기어든 행위는 정말로 미수였을까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">?</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청아</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 항목의 주인공은 곽 한이라는 점에서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">약간 그에게 적당한 견해가 포함되어 있다고 한다면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">?</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아니</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일반적으로 생각해서 적정 연령의 아가씨 머리맡에서 하룻밤 동안 남자가 있고</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아가씨를 좋아한 나머지 밤에 몰래 기어들어왔지만 아무것도 하지 않았다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">같은 변명에서 납득하는 사람이 있을까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">?</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">잠자는 얼굴을 보고 있는 가운데 숙면을 취하는 것도 너무 괴로울 테고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">게다가 이 변명을 듣고</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다음에는 중매인을 부르세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 마음대로 그 자리에서 대처한 건 하인이고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">부모님도 아니었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">게다가 하인을 부르러 간 청아 자신도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하인과 함께 방으로 돌아오고 처음으로 이불 위의 곽 한을 발견했다고 되어있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어째선지 부모님에게 상담하지 않았기 때문에 더 심하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">야한 책을 부모님에게 들킨 남자 중학생이라도 좀 더 궁리해서 변명을 생각해낼 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">숨소리가 들릴 정도로 가까이 있던 곽 한을 깨닫지 못했다는 건 너무 수상하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">백보 양보해서 자신의 이불 위에 곽 한이 있는지 전혀 모르고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">정말로 처음으로 어딘가에 도둑이 있다고 생각해버렸다고 해도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">보통 도둑이 있다고 하면 맨 먼저 부모님을 깨우는 것 정도는 해도 되지 않을까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">당연히 부모님은 나중에 격노했지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이건 이제 사실은 아가씨가 흠집이 있는 것으로 확신해도 전혀 이상한 상황이 아니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">실제로 결혼도 훌륭한 사람을 중개하지 않았다면 못했을 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">한이 이 일을 드러나는 게 두려워서 청아를 협박해 말을 맞췄다면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">청아가 밤에 몰래 들어온 것을 수치스럽다고 생각했다면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하인이 뇌물로 입막음 당했다고 한다면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">……</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">두 사람의 향후를 생각하면서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">굳이 이렇게 해석을 하면 세이가라는 캐릭터는 순식간에 염성</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">艷</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">과 비극성을 띠게 된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">취향이지만 하나의</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">IF</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">설정으로서 생각해보는 만큼 손해는 없을 거라 생각한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미야코 요시카</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그녀가 누구인지를 설명하는 것이 된다면 선택을 재촉 당한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">모노노베 가문의 미야코노이라츠메</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가인</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">歌人</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">인 미야코노요시카</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또는 그 이외다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (SF</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소설의 제도</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">帝都</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이야기에도 그럴듯한 캐릭터는 있는 것 같지만 미검증</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원작 내에서의 대사로부터 본 작품에서는 미야코노이라츠메를 선택했지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 부분은 취미라는 것도 있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요시카는 부적이 없으면 노래를 부른다는 것은 미야코노요시카 설을 보충한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">물론 미야코노이라츠메</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미야코노요시카 라고 하는 것도 좋고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">죽어있으니까 세이가가 조종해서 관직에 올리면 후세에서 나타나도 이상하지 않다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">작품 내에서는 내추럴하게 미야코노이라츠메를 카시와데노미노이라츠메로 삼았지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">당연하게도 이 두 사람에게 상관성은 전혀 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시대가 가깝고 함께 종교전쟁에 관련된 인물이지만 아닌 건 아니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">카시와데노미노이라츠메가 양녀일지도 모른다고 하는 전설은 있지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">거의</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">3</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">면 도중 음악의 제목과 쇼토쿠 태자가 애처에게 말한 말에서 갖다 붙인 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">애초에 미야코노이라츠메는 위서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">偽書</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">라고 취급받는 책에서만 잠깐 나오고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">부모와 결혼 상대와 아이를 낳은 것만 적혀있고 끝인</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">거의 배경 캐릭터</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그렇기에 건드리는 보람이 있다고 말할 수 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그녀도 역시 후토히메의 딸인 가능성이 있기 때문에 토지코노이라츠메와는 의리의 자매 관계라는 것도 생각하지 못할 것도 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">강시에게는 혼</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">魂</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 없는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그저 백</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">魄</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">말하자면 육체적인 감정은 존재한다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">거기에 더해 요시카가 노래를 부른다는 설정에서 기억이라는 것은 또 다른 장소에 있을 것 같다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">감정은 있지만 그것을 총합해서 관리하는 자아가 존재하지 않는다고 할까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">기억의 상기에 의한 행동도 기계적인 부분이 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">대사의</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">고귀한 영혼에 생명을 불어넣은 것이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도 생각해보면 제법 재밌다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미야코노이라츠메나 미야코노요시카 자신은 고귀하다고 할 정도의 신분은 아니었다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다만 그 주위에는 고귀한 이들이 충분히 있을 가능성이 있다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">실제로 토지코</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">후토는 고귀한</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">천황의 유력후보였던 섭정과 그 정처나 어머니니까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요시카의 일인칭이</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">나</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">私</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">외에도</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">우리들</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">我</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">々</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">도 섞여있는 것은 이상하다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어쩌면 강시는 잔뜩 있을지도 모르고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">요시카 자신이 여러 가지 영혼을 통합해서 만들어진 군체적인 존재일지도 모른다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">구문구수에서는 상처가 없다는 점에서 독살을 시사하고 있지만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">영혼을 먹고 회복하는 성질과 세이가의 존재에 의해 요시카의 사인은 알 수 없다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 요시카의 스펠이 포이즌 머더</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">포이즌 레이즈</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 죽지 않는 살인귀로 이어지는 것을 생각해보면</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">독으로 죽고 세이가의 독</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">강시가 되는 약</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">으로 소생한 스토리는 제법 자연스럽다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">또한 영혼만을 잃은 사자</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">[</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">死者</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">]</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">의 강시인 요시카는</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">혼만이 존재하는 사자 즉 망령인 토지코와 대칭된다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그것도 요시카는 영혼을 먹는 존재이다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 두 사람의 관계는 씹으면 씹을수록 맛이 난다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box;">강시라고 하면 성질상 그녀의 생전은 어딘가 비애를 띤 것이 돈다</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box;">하지만 그것을 그녀는 기억하고 있지 않고</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box;">가령 기억하고 있어도 겉으로 표현하지 않을지도 모른다</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box;">신령묘 안에서는 잃어버린 역사의 체현과 같은 캐릭터이다</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. </span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box;">원 소재가 불명료한 자유도의 높음으로</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, </span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box;">바람직한 </span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">key person</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box;">으로 적용시키는 것도 좋다</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 23.4px; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/014.jpg"/></p>
<p></p>
<p class="moreless_fold" id="more2028_9"><span onclick="toggleMoreLess(this, '2028_9','후기','접기'); return false;" style="cursor: pointer;">후기</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"><br/></span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"><br/></span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">치졸한 자료집이지만 읽어주셔서 감사합니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 토지코는 말하지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">원작 및 이 자료집의 문장을 담당한</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">N</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">입니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">갑작스럽지만 태자를 좋아해서 노력해봤습니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 자료집</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">&amp;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아이디어 집은 부디 창작이나 독해의 기본으로 사용해주세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">예를 들면 스토리나 디자인의</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">차적인 이용도 문제없습니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">오리지널을 주장해서 사용하는 듯한 극단적인 경우는 안 됩니다만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">양식의 범위 내라면 허가도 인용명기도 필요 없습니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">다만 그 경우 저자인 저</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(TwitterID:@N_write)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">나</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 토지코는 말하지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">작화인</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">cis</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">씨</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(@cis_ex)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가 작품을 볼 수 있게 해주시면 기쁩니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아니 보고 싶으니까 썼습니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">주세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소녀취 태자님 주세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">엄마 후토 주세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코토지 섹스 주세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">미코요시캉</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시간</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">주세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">참고로 이 책</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">나중에</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">web</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">공개할거라 생각합니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">을 소개해서 퍼트려주시면 더 감사합니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">단순한 복사 붙여넣기 작품의 제작</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 자료집의 복사를 재배포 등</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">문장과 그림 함께 저작권을 침해하는 행위는 금지합니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그리고 타인의 자유로운 신령묘</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">차 창작에 대해 이 책을 내세워</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기 역사의 원 소재랑 다르다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">같은 멋없는 말은 하지 맙시다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">. (</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">중요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">)</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사에 정말로 충실히 하면 모두 아저씨랑 아줌마고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">세이가는 등장도 못하고 끝나버리고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">아무도 못 읽는 옛날말로 얘기해버립니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">차 창작의 재미는 얼마나 정설을 짓밟고 훌륭하게 춤추는 가에도 있다고 생각합니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">애초에 목표로 하는 원전 자체 개찬 편향 과장 투성이니까 엔터테인먼트로서는 바람직한 기술만 반입해도 재밌으면</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">OK</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">입니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">논문을 쓴다고 하시면 이 책은 엄청 도움이 안 된다고 생각하니 그건 그거</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사 공부가 필수인 것 같은 선입관이 생기기 쉬운 신령묘 입니다만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">공부라기보다는 작은 소재 회수라고 생각합니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">그냥 캐릭터 사랑만으로도 충분합니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">귀여움은 정의니까</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사 같은 건 버리고 덤벼들어도 좋습니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">어디까지나</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">+</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">α</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">입니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">하지만 캐릭터의 인물상의 고찰이나</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사상 사실과 관련된 스토리의 설득력을</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">UP</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시키거나 하는 잔기술에는 도움이 된다고 생각해요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">?</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">『</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">소가노 토지코는 말하지 않는다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">』</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">설정집을 겸하고 있고</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이런 저런 역사해설 신령묘</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">차 창작 소재의 한 구체적 예로 들고 싶다라고 말하려는 의도였습니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">「</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 책만 읽으면 신령묘</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">2</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">차 창작은 완벽</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">!</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">」</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">까지는 말하지 않습니다만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">유명한 부분의 역사 소재는 상당히 커버하고 있다고 생각합니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 부근은 자기책임으로 맛있는 소재만 통째로 삼켜주세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">가능하면 만약을 위해 스스로 조사해서</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">!</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">우선 사용할 수 있는 재밌는 소재는 가능한 만큼 담았습니다만</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">여기에 싣지 못한 소재도 잔뜩 있으므로 계속해서 발굴해주세요</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">재미를 중시해서 모았기 때문에 여러모로 미스나 오해가 있을 지도 모르니</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">지적이나 감상 등은 저</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(@N_write)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">로 부탁드립니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">설정 그림의 제작</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">및 비쥬얼 면 중심에</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">,</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">스토리에도 설정 고찰해준</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">cis</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">씨</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(@cis_ex).</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">이 책의 교정</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">역사 기술 체크</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">레이아웃</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">·</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">일부 정보의 제공을 해주신 태자빠 키타유키 씨</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(@k_t_y_k).</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">시험 삼아 읽어주신 미츠와 미히라 씨</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">, N2</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">씨</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 함초롬바탕;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(@N2_Desire), sophistry</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">씨</span><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">(@sophistry_3104).</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">감사합니다</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">.</span></p>
<p class="0" style='box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: "Nanum Gothic", sans-serif; line-height: 23.4px;'><span style="font-family: Gulim, 굴림;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; text-align: right; box-sizing: border-box;">그럼 여러분 보다 좋은 신령묘 창작 라이프를</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 23.4px; text-align: right; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: Gulim, 굴림;">!</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Gulim, 굴림; line-height: 23.4px; text-align: right;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/015.jpg"/></p>
<p></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><img src="{{ site.nasurl }}/ghap/2028/016.jpg"/></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;">[Carcharias!] 소가노 토지코는 말하지 않는다 설정자료집 &amp; 신령묘 아이디어집</p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;"><br/></p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;">허미 쉬펄 갖고 오는 것도 힘들구만.</p>
<p style="text-align: center; clear: none; float: none;">이런 재미없는 작업은 선미즘이라고 출처를 적어야 해.</p>
